  3  /*

SQL> @drop_all.sql
SQL> declare
  2  
  3  cursor c1 is
  4  select 'DROP '||
  5  	    decode(object_type,
  6  	      'PACKAGE SPECIFICATION', 'PACKAGE',
  7  	      'TYPE SPECIFICATION',    'TYPE',
  8  	      object_type)||
  9  	    ' '||
 10  	    object_name sql_statement
 11  from   USER_OBJECTS
 12  where  object_name not in ('DDL_', 'PL');
 13  
 14  n_count				   number := 0;
 15  
 16  begin
 17    for i in 1..5 loop
 18  	 for r1 in c1 loop
 19  	   begin
 20  	     execute immediate r1.sql_statement;
 21  
 22  	     n_count := n_count + 1;
 23  	   exception
 24  	     when OTHERS then
 25  	       null;
 26  	   end;
 27  	 end loop;
 28    end loop;
 29    SYS.DBMS_OUTPUT.put_line(n_count||' objects dropped.');
 30  end;
 31  /
0 objects dropped.

PL/SQL procedure successfully completed.
